  <script>
   (function () {
        var isIPad = (navigator.platform === 'MacIntel' && navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0) || navigator.platform === 'iPad';

        var htmlEscapes = {
            '&': '&amp;',
            '<': '&lt;',
            '>': '&gt;',
            '"': '&quot;',
            "'": '&#39;'
        }
        var reUnescapedHtml = /[&<>"']/g
        var reHasUnescapedHtml = RegExp(reUnescapedHtml.source)
        function _escape(string) {
            return (string && reHasUnescapedHtml.test(string))
                ? string.replace(reUnescapedHtml, function(chr) { htmlEscapes[chr] })
                : (string || '')
        }

        var Loaded = {
            get: function (name) { // @吴律 负责的逻辑
                var arr,
                    reg = new RegExp("(^| )" + name + "=([^;]*)(;|$)");
                if (arr = document.cookie.match(reg)) {
                    return unescape(arr[2]);
                } else {
                    return null;
                }
            },
            mobile: function () {
                return this.get('mobile')
            },
            avatar: function () {
                var userInfo = (window._global || {}).userInfo || {};
                return userInfo.avatar;
            },
            getHtml: function () {
                var html;
                var mobile = this.mobile(); // 获取用户登录态
                var avatar = this.avatar();
                var isMeeting = location.href.indexOf('huiyi') > -1; // 会议登录 @文博 负责的逻辑
                var rightStatus = document.getElementById("right_status")
                var statusBtn = document.getElementById('entryBtn')

                if (mobile) {
                    html = '<li class="intro_header_loaded_common_"><a href="javascript:;"><span id="avatar_common_"';
                    rightStatus.classList.add("isLogin")
                    statusBtn.href = '//www.youzan.com/v2/shop/route'
                    statusBtn.innerText = '进入后台'

                    if (avatar) {
                        avatar = unescape(avatar);
                        html += 'style="background-image:url(' + avatar.replace(/^http:\/\//, 'https://') +
                            ');"';
                    }
                    if (isMeeting) {
                        html +=
                            '></span><a target="_blank" href="https://huiyi.youzan.com/manage"><span id="mobile_common_">' +
                            mobile +
                            '</span></a></a><ul class="intro_header_loaded-menu_"><li><a target="_blank" href="https://huiyi.youzan.com/manage">进入后台</a></li><li><a target="_blank" href="//www.youzan.com/v2/account/personal">帐号设置</a></li><li><a href="//account.youzan.com/logout?redirectUrl=https%3A%2F%2Faccount.youzan.com%2Flogin%3FredirectUrl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fhuiyi.youzan.com%2Fshop%23%2Flist">退出登录</a></li></ul></li>';
                    } else {
                        html +=
                            '></span><a target="_blank" href="//www.youzan.com/v2/shop/route"><span id="mobile_common_">' +
                            mobile +
                            '</span></a></a><ul class="intro_header_loaded-menu_"><li><a target="_blank" href="//www.youzan.com/v2/shop/route">进入后台</a></li><li><a target="_blank" href="//www.youzan.com/v2/account/personal">帐号设置</a></li><li><a href="//account.youzan.com/logout">退出登录</a></li></ul></li>';
                    }
                } else {

                    html =
                        '<div class="btn-contact-us"><a target="_blank" id="ruzhuBtn">联系我们</a></div><div class="intro_header_middle-line"></div><div class="intro_header_btn-login_"><a target="_blank" href="https://account.youzan.com/login">登录</a></div>';
                }
                return html;
            },

            getUrl: function () { // header当前页高亮 @加一 负责的逻辑
                var pathMap = {
                    '/': 0, // value表示header nav索引
                    '/intro/weapp': 1,
                    '/intro/cy': 1,
                    '/intro/huiyi': 1,
                    '/intro/solution/piaowu': 1,
                    '/intro/custom': 1,
                    '/intro/ga': 1,
                    '/intro/media': 1,
                    '/intro/products': 1,
                    '/intro/solution/jiudian': 1,
                    '/intro/wsc': 1,
                    '/v2/index/wxdpc': 2,
                    '/intro/choice': 2,
                    '/intro/guarantee': 2,
                    '/intro/qudao': 3,
                    '/intro/shangmeng': 5,
                    '/intro/shangmeng/activity': 5,
                    '/intro/fuwu': 5,
                    '/intro/gongyi': 5
                }
                var itemIndex = pathMap[window.location.pathname];
                if (!itemIndex && itemIndex !== 0) return;
                var list = document.getElementsByClassName('intro_header_product-center')
                list[itemIndex].className += ' current-highlight' // 根据索引让对应item高亮
            },
            init: function () {
                var nav_list_common_ = document.getElementById('nav_list_contact');
                var html = this.getHtml();
                nav_list_common_.innerHTML += html;
                var rightStatus = document.getElementById('right_status')

                var button = document.getElementById('nav_search_img');
                var input = document.getElementById("nav_input");
                var popElem = document.getElementById("nav_search_pop");
                // 手动模拟click事件的标识位
                var isMousedown = false;
                var BASE_SEARCH_URL = "https://so.youzan.com/?from_source=" + getUrlParameter('from_source') + "&kw=";
                var inPopElem = false;
                var blurElem = document.getElementById('phptpl-blur')
                var dropdown_prodct = document.getElementById('product_dropdown_elem')
                var dropdown_solution = document.getElementById('solution_dropdown_elem')
                var ruzhuBtn = document.getElementById('ruzhuBtn')
                var giftBlock = document.getElementById('consult_phone_wrap')

                function getUrlParameter(name) {
                    name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
                    var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
                    var results = regex.exec(location.search || '');
                    return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                };

                var showPopElem = function () {
                    popElem.classList.add('show')
                    popElem.classList.remove('hidden')
                }

                var hiddenPopElem = function () {
                    popElem.classList.add('hidden')
                    popElem.classList.remove('show')
                }

                var scrollFunc = function () {
                    //  官网的二级导航
                    var secondNav = document.getElementsByClassName("second-js-top")[0];
                    var headerBefore = document.getElementsByClassName("header-before")[0];
                    var phptplHeader = document.getElementsByClassName("phptpl-header")[0];
                    if (secondNav) {
                        headerBefore.hidden = true;
                        phptplHeader.style.position = "relative";
                        phptplHeader.style.boxShadow = "0 0 0 rgba(0,0,0,.08)";
                    }
                }

                function addClass(elem, className) {
                    if(elem) {
                        elem.classList.add(className)
                    }
                }

                function removeClass(elem, className) {
                    if(elem) {
                        elem.classList.remove(className)
                    }
                }

                var currentEl = null
                var isBubbleClick = false
                function bindBlurAnimation(elem, state) {
                    var phptplheader = document.getElementById('phptpl-header')
                    var giftGuide = document.getElementById('gift-guide')

                    if (isIPad) {
                        elem.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                            if (currentEl === event.target) {
                                removeClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                                currentEl = null
                            } else {
                                addClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                                currentEl = event.target
                            }

                            if (isBubbleClick) {
                                isBubbleClick = false
                                removeClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                            }
                        })
                    } else {
                        elem.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(event) {
                            addClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                            var clueCollect = document.getElementById('clues-collect-container')
                            clueCollect && (clueCollect.style.display = 'none')
                            giftGuide && (giftGuide.style.display = 'none')
                            state = false
                        })

                        elem.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(event) {
                            removeClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                            var clueCollect = document.getElementById('clues-collect-container')
                            clueCollect && (clueCollect.style.display = 'block')
                            giftGuide && (giftGuide.style.display = 'block')
                            state = true
                        })
                    }
                }

                function linkWithNoBlur(selector) {
                    // 处理safari > 13.1 连接跳转后毛玻璃不消失问题进行操作
                    if (document.querySelectorAll) {
                        var links = document.querySelectorAll(selector)
                        links.forEach(function(item) {
                            item.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                isBubbleClick = true
                            })
                        })
                    }
                }

                linkWithNoBlur('.intro_header_product-block a')
                linkWithNoBlur('.intro_header_item-solution a')


                setTimeout(function() {
                    bindBlurAnimation(dropdown_prodct, false)
                    bindBlurAnimation(dropdown_solution, false)
                }, 100)

                if (isIPad) {
                    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.getElementsByClassName('intro_header_dropdown-menu-wrapper'), function (ele) {
                        ele.addEventListener('mouseover', function (event) {
                            isBubbleClick = true
                        })
                    });

                    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.getElementsByClassName('product-dropdown-no-blur'), function (ele) {
                        ele.addEventListener('mouseover', function (event) {
                            currentEl = event.target.parentNode
                            removeClass(blurElem, 'show_blur')
                        })
                    });
                }

                // 滚动事件节流
                var timeout = setTimeout(scrollFunc, 300);
                var startTime = Date.parse(new Date);

                //  若有二级导航则取消header顶置，优先使用二级导航置顶
                //  一级导航比二级导航先渲染所以用滚动触发，layout插入的js比二级导航前，直接document获取不到
                window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                    if (timeout !== null) clearTimeout(timeout);
                    var curTime = Date.parse(new Date);
                    if (curTime - startTime >= 30) {
                        scrollFunc();
                        startTime = curTime;
                    } else {
                        timeout = setTimeout(scrollFunc, 30);
                    }
                });

                function throttle(func, wait, mustRun) {
                    var timeout,
                        startTime = new Date();
                
                    return function() {
                        var context = this,
                            args = arguments,
                            curTime = new Date();
                
                        clearTimeout(timeout);
                        if(curTime - startTime >= mustRun){
                            func.apply(context,args);
                            startTime = curTime;
                        }else{
                            timeout = setTimeout(func, wait);
                        }
                    };
                };


                //导航栏滑动固定顶部
                var nav = document.getElementById("header-bottom-wrap");
                var header = document.getElementById('header-container')
                var phpHeader = document.getElementById('phptpl-header')
                var navTop = nav.clientHeight;
                var nowStat = 'total'

                window.addEventListener('scroll', function(){
                    var scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
                    if (scrollTop >= navTop){
                        if (nowStat === 'hidden') return
                        phpHeader.classList.add('header_fixed')
                        nowStat = 'hidden'
                    } else {
                        if(nowStat === 'total') return
                        phpHeader.classList.remove('header_fixed')
                        nowStat = 'total'
                    }   
                })

                var textArr = ["微商城", "电商直播", "微信小程序", "零售", "如何开店"];
                var inputVal = document.getElementById("nav_input");

                var num = 0;
                startMove = function () { //搜索框热词3s更新
                    var timer = setInterval(function() {
                        if (num === 4) {
                            num = 0;
                        } else {
                            inputVal.placeholder = textArr[num];
                            num++;
                        }
                    }, 3000);
                    inputVal.onclick = function(){
                        clearInterval(timer);
                        inputVal.style.color = "#323233";
                    }
                    inputVal.onfocus = function(){
                        inputVal.setAttribute("class","intro_header_nav_input_focus");
                    }
                    inputVal.onblur = function(){
                        inputVal.setAttribute("class","intro_header_nav_input_normal")
                    }
                };
                inputVal.placeholder = textArr[textArr.length - 1]
                startMove()

                button.addEventListener('mousedown', function () {
                    inPopElem = true
                })

                giftBlock && giftBlock.addEventListener("click", function () {  
                    window.openAdvisory && window.openAdvisory();
                })

                ruzhuBtn && ruzhuBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    window.openAdvisory && window.openAdvisory();
                })

                button.addEventListener("mouseup", function () {
                    var hotWordsList = JSON.parse(
                        window.localStorage.getItem("search_hot_words") || "[]"
                    );
                    var keyWord = _escape(input.value || inputVal.placeholder).replace(/ /ig, "");

                    if (keyWord && hotWordsList.indexOf(keyWord) === -1) {
                        hotWordsList.unshift(keyWord);
                        window.localStorage.setItem(
                            "search_hot_words",
                            JSON.stringify(hotWordsList.slice(0, 8))
                        );
                        window.Logger &&
                            window.Logger.log({
                                et: 'custom', // 事件类型
                                ei: 'hover_so_search', // 事件标识
                                en: '公共头搜索词', // 事件名称
                                pt: 'intro', // 页面类型
                                params: {
                                    key_word: keyWord
                                } // 事件参数
                            });
                    }


                    input.value = "";
                    popElem.innerHTML = "";
                    hiddenPopElem()
                    inPopElem = false
                    input.blur()


                    // 这里需要跳转去新的so.youzan.com
                    window.open(BASE_SEARCH_URL + keyWord);
                });

                input.addEventListener("keypress", function (ev) {
                    if (ev.keyCode === 13) {
                        var keyWord = _escape(input.value || inputVal.placeholder).replace(/ /ig, "");
                        var hotWordsList = JSON.parse(
                            window.localStorage.getItem("search_hot_words") || "[]"
                        );

                        if (keyWord && hotWordsList.indexOf(keyWord) === -1) {
                            hotWordsList.unshift(keyWord);
                            window.localStorage.setItem(
                                "search_hot_words",
                                JSON.stringify(hotWordsList.slice(0, 8))
                            );
                            window.Logger &&
                                window.Logger.log({
                                    et: 'custom', // 事件类型
                                    ei: 'hover_so_search', // 事件标识
                                    en: '公共头搜索词', // 事件名称
                                    pt: 'intro', // 页面类型
                                    params: {
                                        key_word: keyWord
                                    } // 事件参数
                                });
                        }

                        window.open(BASE_SEARCH_URL + keyWord);
                    }
                });

                popElem &&
                    popElem.addEventListener("mousedown", function (event) {
                        !isMousedown && (isMousedown = true);
                    });

                popElem && popElem.addEventListener("mouseover", function () {
                    inPopElem = true
                })

                popElem && popElem.addEventListener("mouseleave", function () {
                    inPopElem = false
                })

                popElem && popElem.addEventListener(
                    "mouseup",
                    function (event) {
                        if (!isMousedown || event.target.className === 'func_bar') return;

                        var currElem = event.target;
                        var parentNode = currElem.parentNode;
                        var className = currElem.className;

                        if (parentNode.className === "func_delete") {
                            window.localStorage.clear();
                            popElem.innerHTML = "";
                            hiddenPopElem()
                            isMousedown = true;
                            input.blur()
                            return;
                        }

                        if (className === "func_item") {
                            input.value = _escape(currElem.innerHTML);
                            window.Logger &&
                                window.Logger.log({
                                    et: 'custom', // 事件类型
                                    ei: 'hover_so_search', // 事件标识
                                    en: '公共头搜索词', // 事件名称
                                    pt: 'intro', // 页面类型
                                    params: {
                                        key_word: input.value
                                    } // 事件参数
                                });
                            window.open(BASE_SEARCH_URL + input.value || "");

                            isMousedown = true;
                            input.blur()
                        }
                    },
                    true
                );

                input && input.addEventListener(
                    "blur",
                    function () {
                        if (inPopElem) {
                            input.focus()
                            return
                        }
                        rightStatus.classList.remove("right_status_focus")
                        startMove()

                        setTimeout(function() {
                            popElem.innerHTML = "";
                            hiddenPopElem()
                        }, 10);
                    },
                    false
                );

                input && input.addEventListener("focus", function (event) {
                    var hotWordsList = JSON.parse(
                        window.localStorage.getItem("search_hot_words") || "[]"
                    );
                    rightStatus.classList.add("right_status_focus")
                    window.Logger &&
                        window.Logger.log({
                            et: 'custom',
                            ei: 'so_input_focus_office',
                            en: '官网搜索输入框focus',
                            pt: 'intro',
                        });

                    if (!hotWordsList || !hotWordsList.length) return;

                    var funcBar =
                        '<li class="func_bar"><span>最近搜过</span><span class="func_delete"><img src="//img01.yzcdn.cn/upload_files/2020/07/23/FuC4uiEVdJlWJkCuVUdeGyVffcnd.png" width="18px" height="18px"></img><span class="func_delete_text">清除记录</span></span></li>';
                    var recentItems = hotWordsList.map(function (value) {
                        return "<div class='func_item'>" + _escape(value) + "</div>";
                    });


                    popElem.innerHTML = funcBar + recentItems.join("");
                    showPopElem()

                });

                this.getUrl()
            }
        }
        Loaded.init();
    })()
  </script>
